# Progress Tracker

> Update this file after every meaningful implementation change. This is the only file in `context/` that changes constantly; the others are stable.

## Current Phase

- **✅ Wave 7 Unit 51 complete (2026-05-27)** — visit-bank commercial model + legacy bridge (Group B) + org plans (Group C) + billing ops (Group D).

Verified documents extend Unit 06/Miss Cleo source material; unverified and partially reviewed documents remain behind the `verifiedAt != null` read fence.

Wave 8 Units 43–47 remain paused until the polish gate clears.
- **🔧 Sprint 0 — Login & session trust (P0).** Sprint 0.20 removed MFA entirely (auth is now email + password, with a 4-digit signing PIN for sign-time re-auth), retiring the MFA redirect-loop class of bugs. Remaining work: the login getSession race and session-trust hardening before Sprint A clinical work. **Spec:** [`context/specs/sprint-0-login-first.md`](specs/sprint-0-login-first.md).

## Completed

- **2026-05-30 — Concrete profession + division enforced at every user-creation path.** Fixed a visit-start dead-end: a self-serve org/admin created with `OrgUser.division=MULTI`, `professionType=null`, and `Organization.defaultDivision=null` made `resolveDivisionForNote` throw `no_division_resolvable` (HTTP 422 "Could not derive a note division for this visit") the first time they tried to start a note — and the profile-completion gate only guards `/prepare` + `/capture`, surfaces that exist only *after* a note row exists, so a fresh signup admin had no recovery path. Established the invariant at the row-creation boundary: every recording-capable `OrgUser` (ORG_ADMIN, SITE_ADMIN, CLINICIAN) must carry a concrete `professionType` (not null/OTHER) and concrete `division` (not null/MULTI); VIEWER stays exempt; `Organization.division=MULTI` remains legitimate for multi-discipline clinics (only per-USER values are forced concrete). **Surfaces (commit `0711a3d`):** signup API + form require a concrete profession + division and seed `Organization.defaultDivision` from the founder's division as a resolver safety-net; invite API + admin form `superRefine` requires concrete profession/division for recording roles, persists `Invite.professionType`, and returns field-level issues; invite acceptance copies `Invite.professionType` onto `OrgUser` in both upsert branches; the four org seeds provision admins/site-admins/owner as MD + MEDICAL so they pass by being complete (not by a role bypass); a reactive safety net surfaces a "Complete your profile" link on the start-visit dialog if a division-resolution error ever fires (gate logic unchanged). **Follow-on hardening (2nd commit):** the owner `PeopleCard` roster now filters `user.isDeleted: false` (a soft-deleted membership is a tombstone, not a Deactivated member — mirrors the owner users list + orgs page) which fixed `owner-org-people` counting an orphaned admin tombstone; and the demo/extra-clinician seed upserts now self-heal after billing/deleted-data drift (reactivate + 1y-extend the seat, restore `OrgUser.isActive` + `seatId`, restore the 3 core demo patients to `isDeleted:false`) so the long-lived dev DB stays e2e-green across reseeds. **Live browser walk (real server, authenticated fetch through the actual server paths):** signup with OTHER+MULTI → 400; valid PT/REHAB → 201 with org `division=REHAB`/`defaultDivision=REHAB` and admin OrgUser `ORG_ADMIN`/`REHAB`/`PT`; login → `/home` with no profile gate; site → patient → encounter all HTTP 200, and the minted note resolved **`division=REHAB`, `status=PREPARING` with no 422** (bug fixed end-to-end); invite with OTHER+MULTI → 400, valid invite → 409 `seat_cap_reached` (seat gate firing as designed on the SOLO trial), and accepting an invite persisted `OrgUser` `CLINICIAN`/`REHAB`/`PT`. Throwaway walkthrough org/users were then hard-deleted from the dev DB via an atomic FK-ordered transaction (verified seed corpus intact: 23 orgs / 52 users, `owner@demo.local` present). **Verification:** `npm run lint` 0 errors (10 pre-existing warnings); `npm run typecheck` clean; `npm test` 1198 passed; `npm run build` ✓ compiled; `npm run e2e` 71 passed / 2 skipped / 0 failed. **Three-lens:** Clinician — a new provider can no longer reach the exam room in a state where the note's division can't be derived; division is set deterministically from their profession. Medicare Compliance Officer — every note carries a concrete clinical division from creation, so medical-necessity/skilled-care framing and division-scoped templates apply from visit one with no MULTI/null ambiguity. Insurance Auditor — division provenance is traceable to a concrete `professionType` captured at the user-creation boundary, persisted on `OrgUser`, and carried onto the note, reconstructable end to end.

- **2026-05-30 — Deleted-data recovery workflows (owner restore + org-admin deactivate/reactivate).** Completes the soft-delete story with owner-only recovery and org-scoped lifecycle controls. **Owner restore:** a new owner-only `/owner/deleted-data` screen (force-dynamic, AlertDialog-gated) lists soft-deleted orgs and users with deleted date, deleted-by, original id, retained counts, and — for anonymized users — the original email/name reconstituted from an owner-only, access-audited recovery ledger (`DeletedRecordLedger`). Restoring an org (`POST /api/owner/orgs/[id]/restore`) un-hides it and reactivates exactly the memberships/seats recorded in its ledger (skipping users still soft-deleted); restoring a user (`POST /api/owner/users/[id]/restore`) reconstitutes identity from the ledger, reactivates memberships in non-deleted orgs, clamps any `PLATFORM_OWNER` original role down to `NONE`, and 409s on email collision or a missing ledger. Viewing the screen and every restore are audited (`PLATFORM_DELETED_DATA_VIEWED`, `PLATFORM_ORG_RESTORED`, `PLATFORM_USER_RESTORED`). **Org-admin lifecycle:** org admins cannot delete an org; they can only deactivate/reactivate users in their OWN org (`PATCH /api/admin/users/[id]`, org-scoped `findFirst`). Deactivation frees the held seat (nulls `seatId` + writes a `SeatTransfer` "Freed on deactivation"), wipes sessions, and audits `USER_DEACTIVATED`; the `/admin/users` table filters active vs deactivated cohorts. **Migration:** `20260607000000_owner_soft_delete` (Organization/User soft-delete fields + `DeletedRecordLedger`); `npx prisma migrate deploy` and `npx prisma db seed` passed locally (seed adds a deleted org, a ledger-anonymized deleted user, and a dedicated `deactivate-me@demo.local` member for e2e). **Verification:** `npx prisma generate`, `npx prisma validate`, focused restore + admin-limit tests, `npm test` (138 files / 1198 tests), `npm run typecheck`, `npm run lint` (10 pre-existing warnings), `npm run build` (✓ compiled), and the `owner-deleted-data` + `admin-user-deactivate` Playwright specs (4 passed) all passed.

- **2026-05-30 — Owner soft-delete controls for organizations and users.** Platform owners can now delete organizations from `/owner/orgs` and users from `/owner/users` through AlertDialog-gated destructive controls. Deletion is operational soft-delete, not clinical-record purge: org deletion hides the org, deactivates users/seats, clears invites, and retains clinical/audit history; user deletion anonymizes identity, removes sessions/reset tokens, deactivates memberships, removes credential/chat/cache rows tied to their OrgUser ids where safe, and protects PLATFORM_OWNER accounts. Access gates now re-check deleted users/orgs so stale sessions cannot keep working. **Migration:** `20260607000000_owner_soft_delete`; `npx prisma migrate deploy` and `npx prisma db seed` passed locally. **Verification:** `npx prisma generate`, `npx prisma validate`, focused owner-delete tests, `npm test` (136 files / 1184 tests), `npm run typecheck`, `npm run lint` (10 pre-existing warnings), and `npm run build` passed.

- **2026-05-30 — Home clinical data quality soft-delete filter.** The `/home` dashboard now excludes soft-deleted patients from patient-linked schedule, draft, follow-up, document-review, and verified-document-count queries. This keeps the Clinical data quality card from linking to `/patients/[id]` rows that correctly 404 because `Patient.isDeleted = true`. **Verification:** `npm run typecheck` passed; `npm run lint` passed with 10 pre-existing warnings.

- **2026-05-29 — Chart-mode patient-context medication reference bridge.** Added `lookupMedicationReference` as a chart-safe Copilot tool so Miss Cleo can answer patient-context reference questions like "given this patient's age/kidney function, what is the usual losartan dose?" without switching to Research mode. The tool accepts only a medication name, returns curated DailyMed-backed losartan adult-hypertension dosing guidance, and leaves unsupported medications as an empty reference result rather than letting chart mode invent dosing. Chart mode prompt now requires patient facts and general reference facts to be separated, cited separately, and phrased as clinician-review guidance rather than autonomous medication-change recommendations. `lookupPatientDemographics` now returns `ageYears`, verified uploaded documents preload for dose/renal questions, and the Chart tab empty-state examples include patient-context losartan dosing. **Verification:** focused tests passed 31/31; `npm run typecheck` passed; `npm run lint` passed with the same 11 warnings; `npm run build` passed; `npm test` passed 132 files / 1165 tests.

- **2026-05-29 — Unit 52 page-addressable document text complete.** Added `ExternalContextDocumentPage` as the searchable page-text layer for uploaded documents, with worker writes from router/OCR page text and lazy backfill for already verified documents. `lookupVerifiedExternalContext` now accepts `pageNumber` and returns verified page text plus page-scoped text matches; Miss Cleo preloads verified documents for page/searchable-document questions and answers direct page requests without an LLM call. Local John Alvarez verification: the existing 40-page verified upload has 40 page rows, and `show me page 5 of the scanned document` returns page 5 medication-reconciliation text from the verified document source. **Verification:** `npx prisma validate` passed; `npx prisma generate` passed; `npm run typecheck` passed; `npm run lint` passed with the same 11 warnings; focused Unit 52/Cleo page tests passed; `npm test` passed 131 files / 1161 tests; `npm run build` passed; `PLAYWRIGHT_SKIP_WEBSERVER=1 E2E_BASE_URL=http://localhost:3000 npm run e2e` passed 66/66. **Migration note:** default dev DB migration history remains divergent, so the local DB table was applied as an additive-only table without reset or data-loss push; the Prisma migration file exists for clean/non-divergent environments.

- **2026-05-29 — Unit 52 follow-up complete: clinical file ingestion router V2 + Textract deployment wiring.** Added a strict baseline/benchmark report pair for the zero known regression gate (`reports/ingestion-router-v2-baseline.md`, `reports/ingestion-router-v2-benchmark.md`) plus feature-flagged router V2 behind `OMNISCRIBE_FILE_ROUTER_V2`. Text-based PDFs now extract the embedded text layer directly and skip OCR/vision page batching; sparse PDFs route to an OCR-provider abstraction and use AWS Textract async OCR in deployed environments when `OCR_PROVIDER=textract`; DOCX/RTF/TXT/CSV/XLSX/XML/JSON parse directly; single image/lab screenshot uploads remain on the existing Unit 52 fast vision path. The Textract provider uses the already-uploaded private S3 document object, relies on normal AWS region/env configuration and the worker IAM role, supports optional Textract SNS notification, output, and KMS env vars, and is included in `scripts/verify-providers.ts` as a deployment config check. The external-context worker creates one full-document review batch for V2 text routes, preserving clinician review and final `verifiedAt != null` as the downstream Cleo/brief/scribe read gate. The mandatory 40-page John Alvarez synthetic PDF fixture was added under `tests/fixtures/ingestion/`; benchmark output confirmed `detected_route=pdf_text_layer`, `ocr_used=no`, 40 pages, 87,808 extracted chars, 10 ms pre-LLM extraction, and pass. **Verification:** baseline before changes passed `npx prisma validate`, `npm run typecheck`, `npm run lint` (11 pre-existing warnings), `npm test` after local Docker access (125 files / 1136 tests), and `npm run build` after removing generated `.next/node_modules/.DS_Store` and allowing Google Fonts network fetch. Final focused tests passed 18/18 for OCR/router/worker coverage after SNS option hardening; `npm run typecheck` passed; `npm run lint` passed with the same 11 warnings; `npm run benchmark:ingestion` passed and wrote the benchmark report; `npm test` passed 128 files / 1152 tests; `npx prisma validate` passed; `npm run build` passed. **Risks:** live Textract OCR was not exercised locally because it requires deployed AWS credentials/S3 object access and starts a billable job; optional scanned/image/DOCX/CSV benchmark fixtures were missing and skipped; default local Prisma migration divergence remains pre-existing; the current Textract path can emit SNS notifications but still polls in-worker and can later move to SQS/Lambda or delayed BullMQ completion handling for long jobs.

- **2026-05-29 — Unit 52 follow-up complete: batch-based document extraction + clinician batch review.** Added `ExternalContextExtractionBatch` and `PARTIAL_EXTRACTION_REVIEW` so long documents process in 5-page batches up to a 100-page cap. The extraction worker now creates page ranges, extracts one batch through the existing LLM image abstraction, pauses for clinician review/correction, and only continues after `POST /api/patients/[id]/external-context/[ecId]/batches/[batchId]/review` marks the batch reviewed. The final reviewed batch merges vetted batch payloads into document-level OCR/extraction and leaves the row at `EXTRACTED` for separate final document verification; only final verification sets `verifiedAt` and makes the row visible to briefs/Cleo. Sign-time re-auth is now the 4-digit **signing PIN** (`User.signingPinHash` + unlock window via `/api/auth/pin/*`, from the earlier signing-PIN MVP, migration `20260518195957`); admin-initiated recovery is "Send password reset". This **supersedes** the MFA build in **Unit 01** and the admin MFA-reset in **Unit 08**, and **moots decisions D2/D9** (always-required MFA policy + seeded TOTP test vector) — those historical entries below are retained as record. **This session's cleanup:** (1) removed a dangling admin **"Reset authenticator"** dropdown in `admin/users/_components/row-actions.tsx` that still POSTed to the deleted `/api/admin/users/[id]/reset-mfa` (404 for any admin who clicked it); (2) aligned the canonical living docs (architecture, project-overview, code/ui/copy-standards, this tracker's header), every `specs/` file (with a "Superseded (Sprint 0.20)" banner on `01-foundation-auth-tenant.md` whose body is kept as history), all `journeys/`, and `references/` + the HTML mockup to the password+PIN reality; (3) marked the `MFA_*` `AuditAction` values legacy in `src/lib/audit/actions.ts` (retained, never-rename, so historical `AuditLog` rows still resolve); (4) fixed a live invite-sheet string ("set up their authenticator" → "set their password and signing PIN"). **Verify:** `npm run typecheck` clean; `npm test` 1121/1121 passing; ESLint clean on touched files; repo grep shows zero live MFA code references (remaining hits are historical-log entries, the spec-01 superseded body, and accurate "no MFA / replaced re-MFA" statements). **Three-lens:** Compliance/Auditor — audit-action history preserved (legacy enum kept, not deleted); the changelog now records the removal instead of implying MFA still ships. Sort order in the Seats list now puts admins first, unassigned seats last. New e2e spec `e2e/owner-org-people.spec.ts` (2 tests, both passing) verifies the People + Seats role pills render against the seed org. Also fixed an ESLint hygiene bug: added `**/.next/**` + `.claude/**` to `eslint.config.mjs` ignores so nested build outputs in parallel-agent worktrees stop emitting 1172 spurious "errors" — `npm run lint` now exits 0. **Verify**: `npm run typecheck` clean; `npm run lint` 0 errors / 12 pre-existing warnings; `npm test` 1121/1121 passing; `npm run e2e` 63/63 passing. **Three-lens**: Compliance — owners can now identify the responsible admin in one glance (escalation trail clearer); Auditor — owner-side roster is now coherent with the admin-side `/admin/users` view, no PHI exposed; Clinician — non-clinical surface, no impact on patient flows.
