- **2026-05-24 — Sprint pre-sign-followup-suggest (backend foundation).** Stacked on top of the 2026-05-23 hotfix (PR #120). Spec locked via walkthrough; six design questions answered (decisions table in [`context/specs/sprint-0-presign-followup-suggest.md`](specs/sprint-0-presign-followup-suggest.md)). Backend foundation slice shipped this session:
  - **Schema** (additive only): `FollowUpStatus.PROPOSED` enum value prepended; three nullable provenance columns on `FollowUp` (`proposedSourceText`, `proposedExtractorVersion`, `proposedFromHash`); new compound index `(originNoteId, status)`. Migration `20260527000000_pre_sign_followup_suggest` hand-written (`npx prisma migrate dev` failed due to local-DB / branch divergence — production migrations apply normally; reviewer rebases onto main+PR120 then resets local shadow DB).
  - **`PresignFollowupSuggester` service** (`src/services/brief/PresignFollowupSuggester.ts`): reuses the post-sign `FollowupExtractor` via a new `extractFromPlanContent` method (refactored — old `extractFromFinalJson` now wraps it). Loads the draft note, resolves Plan section via `template.sectionSchema` + `draftJson` keying, computes `sha256(planContent)` for idempotency, supersedes any existing PROPOSED rows (`dropReason='plan_changed_superseded'`) BEFORE writing the new set so the /review UI always sees ≤ one suggestion set aligned with the current Plan. Accepted (OPEN) rows are never touched. Per-row `FOLLOWUP_PROPOSAL_PROPOSED` audit metadata captures the extractor version + planHash + textLength.
  - **POST `/api/notes/[id]/presign-followup-suggest`** (`src/app/api/notes/[id]/presign-followup-suggest/route.ts`): NOTE_REVIEW-gated; org-scoped on the note; rate-limited to 6 extractions per note per 60s using the audit log as the counter (Redis-free; sufficient for the OQ-3 5s-debounce cadence ceiling). Body `{ force?: true }` bypasses the planHash cache for the manual-button path. Returns `{ status: 'created' | 'cached', proposalCount, planHash, ... }`.
  - **Sign-time auto-DROP hook** (`src/app/api/notes/[id]/sign/route.ts`): inside the existing sign transaction (atomic with `Note.status = SIGNED`), `FollowUp.updateMany` flips all PROPOSED rows for the just-signed note to DROPPED with `dropReason='unreviewed_at_sign'`. Audit `FOLLOWUP_PROPOSALS_AUTO_DROPPED_AT_SIGN` with count. Guarantees unreviewed Cleo suggestions never leak to the next visit (Rule 24 compliance).
  - **Audit-action additions**: `FOLLOWUP_PROPOSAL_PROPOSED`, `FOLLOWUP_PROPOSAL_ACCEPTED`, `FOLLOWUP_PROPOSAL_DROPPED`, `FOLLOWUP_PROPOSALS_SUPERSEDED`, `FOLLOWUP_PROPOSALS_AUTO_DROPPED_AT_SIGN` in `src/lib/audit/actions.ts`.
  - **Rule 20 amendment** in `context/architecture.md`: narrow carve-out documented — PresignFollowupSuggester (and only that one extractor channel) MAY read DRAFT Plan content; outputs are PROPOSED-only; every transition audited.
  - **Deferred to next session**: accept/drop endpoints (`POST /api/follow-ups/[id]/accept`), UI changes (two-section card with per-row triage + auto-refresh + cursor protection), post-sign Jaccard de-dup, full test suite. The foundation lands now; the user-facing pieces follow.

- **2026-05-23 — Hotfix: brief-generation reliability (snapshot strip unblock).** Snapshot strip stayed empty for every signed-note flow because `NoteBrief` rows were never being written: BullMQ retried `note-brief:{noteId}` three times for each note and gave up, audit log captured only `errorClass: "Error"` (the `err.message` was discarded), and no `BRIEF_GENERATED` event ever followed `NOTE_BRIEF_ENQUEUED`. Replaying the worker against Robert Hays' notes via `scripts/diagnose-brief-error.ts` surfaced TWO stacked bugs:
  1. **Sonnet 4.5 wraps JSON in ```` ```json … ``` ```` fences** even with `jsonMode: true` + explicit "no markdown fences" in the system prompt. Four parsers in the codebase already strip the fence (`ai-generation/handler.ts`, `FlagAnalyzer.ts`, `copilot/agent.ts`, `copilot/case-router.ts`); four others were missing the strip — `BriefGenerator.parseBriefOutput` (threw loudly), `FollowupExtractor.parseExtraction` (silently returned `{ items: [] }`), `post-sign-artifacts.parseArtifact` (silently fell to stub placeholder), and `copilot/draft-tools.parseModelDraftJson` (silently returned null). Centralized the strip into a new helper `src/lib/llm/strip-json-fence.ts` (12 unit tests covering fenced/unfenced/CRLF/truncated/whitespace variants), refactored all 8 call sites to use it, deleted the local duplicates.
  2. **`BriefGenerator` `maxTokens: 1500` was too low** for a real REHAB visit. Sonnet returned exactly 1500 output tokens and the response ended mid-string with no closing `]`/`}`. Bumped to 4096 (matches the Bedrock SDK default the underlying client falls back to elsewhere). Both Sonnet attempts and the Haiku fallback bumped together so neither path truncates.
  Also patched `src/workers/note-brief/handler.ts` to write `errorMessage` (truncated to 600 chars) into `BRIEF_GENERATION_FAILED` audit metadata so the next silent failure is debuggable from the audit log alone. Verified end-to-end: `BriefGenerator.generate()` against Robert's most recent signed note now succeeds on attempt 1 with `objectiveMeasureCount: 9`. Existing notes whose briefs already exhausted retries (Robert's 3) will not auto-recover; either re-sign a note or invoke a manual re-enqueue (no admin endpoint built yet). Diagnostic script kept under `scripts/diagnose-brief-error.ts` as a permanent replay tool.

- **2026-05-22 — Sprint 0.18: Miss Cleo — proactive nudges** (`feat(sprint-0.18): cleo-proactive-nudges`). **First sprint where Cleo *initiates* the conversation.**
  - **Spec**: `context/specs/sprint-0-cleo-proactive-nudges.md`. Promotes the patterns the Sprint-0.14/0.16/0.17 detectors already emit (via `CopilotPatientState.observedPatternsJson`) into glanceable, dismissible, source-cited nudge cards at the two moments the clinician can actually act on them — the patient chart and the visit-prepare screen.
  - **Schema migration** — `prisma/migrations/20260525000000_sprint_0_18_cleo_nudges`. Four new enums (`CleoNudgeKind` × 6 values, `CleoNudgePriority` HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW, `CleoNudgeStatus` 6-state machine, `CleoNudgeSurface` CHART/VISIT_PREPARE/BOTH). New `CleoNudge` table with 7 FKs (Organization + Patient + OrgUser as owners; User × 3 for dismiss/snooze/act lifecycle authorship) + 4 indexes including the compound unique `(clinicianOrgUserId, patientId, kind, sourcePatternSnapshotHash)` that anchors the upsert dedup path (decision 1). Additive only; `npx prisma db seed` clean (rule 4).
  - **Pure rule-based generator** (`src/services/copilot/nudge-generator.ts`): emits `CleoNudgeCandidate[]` from `observedPatternsJson` + a bundle of Sprint-0.17 non-transient write-back failures. Six per-kind mappers; NO LLM calls in the nudge pathway (decision 11 — the anti-spam discipline). Snapshot hash per kind embeds an *escalation axis* so re-detecting the same logical signal stays one logical nudge but ESCALATION (recert days-until-due crossing a band; PHQ-9 latest value changing; writeback `failureCount` incrementing; goal-stalled days-since crossing a 7-day bucket) yields a NEW hash → a NEW row (decision 3a — an escalating clinical signal must not be silenced by a stale dismissal). 26 unit tests covering all six kinds + stable-hash idempotency + escalation paths + defensive empty/unknown-kind handling + the no-PHI-leakage assertion (CREATE path NEVER consults `existingCondition.icd`).
  - **Pure selector** (`src/services/copilot/nudge-selector.ts`): given candidates + existing rows + the latest observed patterns + a target surface, returns `{surfaced, expired}`. Per-kind cooldown table (RECERT=1d, CASE_FHIR_STATUS_DRIFT=3d, FHIR_WRITEBACK_FAILED_PERMANENT=1d, MEASURE_TREND=14d, GOAL_STALLED=14d, TOPIC=7d — decision 3). Auto-expiry (decision 8): rows whose underlying pattern is gone are returned in `expired` for the read endpoint to batch-flip to EXPIRED + audit. Per-surface cap of 3 (decision 4 — Hick's law). Sort by (priority DESC, proposedAt ASC). Surface filter via `eligibleSurfaces` (BOTH passes anywhere). 20 exhaustive tests covering dedup + cooldown + snooze + auto-expire + priority sort + cap + tie-breaker + hash-collision safety + terminal-state safety.
  - **State-builder integration** (`src/services/copilot/state-builder.ts`): `observedPatternsJson` schema gains `'fhir_writeback_failed_permanent'`. New pure `detectFhirWritebackFailedPermanent` exported. `buildStateProjections` loads `FhirWriteBackProposal` rows with `status=FAILED + failureKind∈(PERMANENT,CONFLICT)` and emits a pattern entry per row. `CLEO_STATE_GENERATOR_VERSION` bumped to `'cleo-state-v4'` so existing rows refresh on next event.
  - **Worker integration** (`src/workers/cleo-state/handler.ts`): after the state upsert, `generateAndPersistNudges` pulls non-transient write-back failures, calls the generator, runs a per-candidate `findUnique` → `create` (create-or-skip semantics — never re-audits an existing logical nudge), and emits `CLEO_NUDGE_PROPOSED` per CREATED row OUTSIDE any swallowing try-catch (rule 8). Rides the existing 5-minute coalesce jobId — NO new BullMQ queue (decision 12 + rule 18). Returns `{nudgeProposedCount}` for the job result. 6 new worker tests covering happy-path, idempotency, escalation, zero-candidate (backward compat), writeback-failure pickup, and rule-8 audit-throw propagation.
  - **State-machine API** — four new routes under `/api/nudges/[id]/`:
    - `dismiss/route.ts`: PROPOSED|SHOWN → DISMISSED + `CLEO_NUDGE_DISMISSED` audit with `surface` metadata. Idempotent on already-DISMISSED; 409 on ACTED/EXPIRED.
    - `snooze/route.ts`: validates `until` (must be future + ≤30d); flips to SNOOZED + `CLEO_NUDGE_SNOOZED` audit with `snoozeUntilIso`. The read-time filter re-surfaces once now ≥ snoozeUntil — no scheduled job.
    - `act/route.ts`: PROPOSED|SHOWN|SNOOZED → ACTED + `CLEO_NUDGE_ACTED` audit carrying the categorical `affordanceSlug` (decision 7 — the auditor lens distinguishes "open-reconcile-flow" from "review-failed-writeback" instead of a generic 'open'). Body's `affordanceSlug` is Zod-validated against the 5-slug enum; unknown slugs → 400. Idempotent on already-ACTED.
    - `shown/route.ts`: stamps `shownAt` (once) + promotes PROPOSED→SHOWN + emits `CLEO_NUDGE_SHOWN`. Idempotent via `shownAt IS NOT NULL` guard. Called by the NudgeCard component's first-mount effect (decision 5 — "was it actually seen" needs the render lifecycle, not the server projection). 22 API tests across the four routes — happy paths, 404, 409, idempotency (decision 5 + 7), bad-request validation.
  - **Page-level loader** (`src/services/copilot/load-eligible-nudges.ts`): reads the per-(patient × clinician) `CopilotPatientState`, the open `CleoNudge` rows, the latest `FhirWriteBackProposal` failures; runs the pure selector; applies the read-time expiry sweep (decision 8 — batch UPDATE + per-row `CLEO_NUDGE_EXPIRED` audit outside any swallowing try-catch); projects surfaced rows into `NudgeCardData` for the UI. Each kind's projection composes a PHI-bearing label + subtitle + a deep-link `affordanceHref` from the snapshot JSON. Returns `[]` when no projection state exists — decision 10 backward compat.
  - **UI components** (`src/components/cleo/`):
    - `nudge-card.tsx` — single-card surface. Priority chip routes through `<StatusBadge>` variants (HIGH→warning, MEDIUM→info, LOW→neutral; rule 23). Affordance button uses per-slug labels (decision 7). On first mount fires `POST /api/nudges/[id]/shown` with a `useRef` guard so remounts don't re-audit (decision 5). Act handler POSTs `/act` then navigates via `next/navigation` `router.push(affordanceHref)`. Dismiss + snooze pipe through the dropdown menu (rule 22 — no `<AlertDialog>` for non-destructive reversible actions).
    - `nudge-dismiss-menu.tsx` — small dropdown with Dismiss / Snooze 1d / Snooze 7d (decision 6 + "out of scope" — custom durations deferred).
    - `chart-nudge-stack.tsx` — default-collapsed "Miss Cleo notes N things" pill, expanding to compact NudgeCards. Lives ADJACENT to the active-case hero (not inside it). Decision 10: empty list renders nothing.
    - `prepare-nudge-block.tsx` — always-expanded list above the recording controls on `/prepare/[noteId]`. Same backward-compat empty-state.
  - **Page wiring**:
    - `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/page.tsx`: loads `chartNudges` via `loadEligibleNudgesForSurface({surface:'CHART'})` and threads them into `PatientChartTabs`. Decision 10 — zero load when no viewer orgUserId (defense in depth).
    - `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/_components/patient-chart-tabs.tsx`: renders `<ChartNudgeStack>` above `<CasesPanel>` inside the Cases tab (only when cases are present — the chart hero pattern already gates on this).
    - `src/app/(clinical)/prepare/[noteId]/page.tsx`: loads `prepareNudges` via the same loader and renders `<PrepareNudgeBlock>` above the recording CTA.
  - **Audit (6 new actions)** — `CLEO_NUDGE_PROPOSED`, `_SHOWN`, `_DISMISSED`, `_SNOOZED`, `_ACTED`, `_EXPIRED`. All PHI-free (decision 9): metadata is `{ nudgeId, kind, priority, ... , personaVersion: 'miss-cleo-v1' }`; never the rendered label string (the label can be reconstructed from `sourcePatternSnapshotJson` at audit-replay if ever needed). `_DISMISSED` + `_SHOWN` carry `surface` (CHART vs VISIT_PREPARE) so the analytics lens can distinguish dismissal locations. `_SNOOZED` carries `snoozeUntilIso`. `_ACTED` carries `affordanceSlug` (decision 7 — the categorical record of which path the clinician chose).
  - **Backward compatibility (decision 10 — verified)**: patients with no `CopilotPatientState` row → `loadEligibleNudgesForSurface` returns `[]` → both surfaces render nothing. Zero-pattern + zero-failure inputs to the generator → zero candidates → zero rows → zero `CLEO_NUDGE_*` audits. The Sprint-0.16/0.17 chart hero + visit-prepare tests pass unchanged (with no test-mock changes required, because the new prisma touchpoints default to empty arrays / null when not mocked). Verified by the dedicated "zero patterns + zero writeback failures → zero nudges + zero audits" worker test.
  - **Files** (new): `prisma/migrations/20260525000000_sprint_0_18_cleo_nudges/migration.sql`; `src/services/copilot/{nudge-generator,nudge-selector,load-eligible-nudges}.ts`; `src/app/api/nudges/[id]/{dismiss,snooze,act,shown}/route.ts`; `src/components/cleo/{nudge-card,nudge-dismiss-menu,chart-nudge-stack,prepare-nudge-block}.tsx`; `test/services/copilot/{nudge-generator,nudge-selector}.test.ts`; `test/api/nudges-{dismiss,snooze,act,shown}.test.ts`; `test/components/{nudge-card,chart-nudge-stack}.test.tsx`.
  - **Files** (modified): `prisma/schema.prisma`; `src/services/copilot/state-builder.ts`; `src/workers/cleo-state/handler.ts`; `src/lib/audit/actions.ts`; `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/page.tsx`; `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/_components/patient-chart-tabs.tsx`; `src/app/(clinical)/prepare/[noteId]/page.tsx`; `test/workers/cleo-state-handler.test.ts`.
  - **Verify**: `npm run typecheck` clean; `npx eslint <touched files>` clean on touched files (2 pre-existing warnings in patient-chart-tabs.tsx unchanged); `REDIS_URL="" DATABASE_URL="" npx vitest run` → 787 tests in 82 files (was 698 baseline + 26 generator + 20 selector + 22 API + 15 component + 6 worker extension = 89 net; 12 integration files still skipping cleanly under the unset-env mirror of CI); `npx prisma generate` + `npx prisma db seed` clean.
  - **Three-lens**: **Clinician** — Cleo graduates from "answers your questions" to "lets you know what to look at." The pill is glanceable; nudges are dismissible in one tap; the affordance takes you to the screen where YOU decide. The visit-prepare surface is the highest-leverage place to learn about a patient's continuity story — Cleo doesn't waste it on noise (per-surface cap of 3; per-kind cooldowns; no LLM-generated nudges; deterministic dedup via the unique-key contract). **Compliance** — every nudge is sourced: the `sourcePatternSnapshotJson` on each row is the exact data the detector saw at the moment the nudge was generated. Combined with the lifecycle audit chain (PROPOSED → SHOWN → ACTED/DISMISSED/SNOOZED/EXPIRED), any compliance question ("did the system inform the clinician about the drift?") becomes a one-join query (`WHERE patientId = ? AND kind = 'CASE_FHIR_STATUS_DRIFT' AND status IN ('SHOWN','ACTED')`). **Auditor** — the affordance slug records WHICH path the clinician chose ("open-reconcile-flow" vs "review-failed-writeback" vs categorical Dismiss). Auditing "did the clinician engage with the system's signals" becomes a categorical question, not a narrative one. The expiry path means stale nudges never linger unaddressed in the audit log — every row is either acted-on, dismissed, snoozed, or naturally expired by the read-time sweep.
  - **Out of scope** (deferred): per-clinician nudge tuning sliders; org-level nudge analytics surface; push/email/SMS off-platform notifications; new pattern detectors beyond the six already in place; nudge merging (two related signals stay as two separate nudges this sprint); custom snooze durations beyond 1d/7d.

- **2026-05-22 — Sprint 0.17: FHIR Phase D₃ — Case → Condition write-back** (`feat(sprint-0.17): fhir-writeback`). **First sprint that mutates the EHR.**
  - **Spec**: `context/specs/sprint-0-fhir-writeback.md`. Builds additively on Sprint 0.15 (read direction — `mirrorsFhirConditionId`) and Sprint 0.16 (drift detection + the `reconcile` action). Three flows ship: create-on-open (open-new / open-new-from-condition), patch-on-status-change (close-case / reopen-case), patch-on-ICD-change (update-case-icd / open-new-case).
  - **Schema migration** — `prisma/migrations/20260524000000_sprint_0_17_fhir_writeback`. Three new enums (`FhirWriteBackOperation`, `FhirWriteBackStatus`, `FhirWriteBackFailureKind`) + new `FhirWriteBackProposal` table (one row per proposed EHR write; unique `idempotencyKey`; lineage FKs to `CaseRouterRun` + `CaseFhirDriftLog` + Org/Case/Patient/User; outcome columns; 5 indexes). Three new columns on `OrgEhrConnection`: `writebackEnabled` (Boolean, default FALSE — decision 10 backward compat), `writebackEnabledAt`, `writebackEnabledByUserId`. Additive only; `npx prisma db seed` clean (rule 4).
  - **Three-gate opt-in (decision 1 — non-negotiable)**: (1) org-level `OrgEhrConnection.writebackEnabled` (admin click on the new `WritebackToggle` settings card), (2) per-write clinician click in the review-panel inline section, (3) `<AlertDialog>` confirmation modal with the payload summary. No code path bypasses any gate. Verified by accept-endpoint tests for the disabled path + the worker re-check at job pickup.
  - **Source-of-truth invariant (decision 3)**: the case mutation commits FIRST inside the accept-endpoint tx; the `FhirWriteBackProposal` row + the `FHIR_WRITEBACK_PROPOSED` audit are inserted in the SAME tx so a throw rolls everything back together. The proposal sits at `PROPOSED` until the clinician approves; the actual FHIR write is a follow-on by the worker. A failed EHR write NEVER undoes OS state — the case stays ACTIVE / CLOSED / new-ICD'd as resolved; the proposal moves to FAILED for clinician review.
  - **Pure write-back service** (`src/services/fhir/case-writeback.ts`): `buildCreateConditionPayload` (FHIR R4 Condition with ICD-10-CM coding + `clinicalStatus` mapped from OS case.status + the `omniscribe-origin` extension stamping the OS case id on every CREATE), `buildPatchOperations` (minimal RFC-6902 JSON Patch — `replace /clinicalStatus` and/or `replace /code`; deterministic order; collapses FHIR-side `remission/relapse` onto active/resolved before diffing), `proposeWriteBack` (orchestrator — picks CREATE vs PATCH from `mirrorsFhirConditionId`, generates a `cuid2` `idempotencyKey`, returns null for no-op PATCHes). 30+ unit tests in `test/services/fhir/case-writeback.test.ts` covering CREATE / PATCH-status / PATCH-ICD / PATCH-combined / idempotency-key shape + uniqueness / all defense-in-depth rejections (missing `fhirPatientId`, missing ICD, CANCELLED/PENDING_ROUTER guards, no-FHIR-side-leakage assertion).
  - **FHIR client extension** (`src/services/fhir/patient-client.ts`): two new methods — `createCondition` (POST /Condition, returns `{ok, fhirId, versionId}` or `{ok:false, failureKind, status, message}` — never throws — rule 8 requirement) and `patchCondition` (PATCH /Condition/{id} with `If-Match: W/"<version>"` and `Content-Type: application/json-patch+json` per decision 5/6; same never-throws contract). Both honor `X-Request-Id` for vendor-side idempotency (Epic + Cerner; OS-side `idempotencyKey` unique constraint is the fallback). HTTP-status taxonomy mapper (`classifyFhirHttpStatus`): 412 → CONFLICT, 5xx / 408 / 429 → TRANSIENT, all other 4xx → PERMANENT (decision 7). Bearer tokens + URL-embedded creds stripped from `failureMessage` before persisting. Stub-mode synthesizes deterministic ids so dev exercises the full pipeline without a real EHR.
  - **BullMQ worker** (`src/workers/fhir-writeback/handler.ts` + `src/workers/fhir-writeback.worker.ts`): registered at concurrency=2 (EHR write QPS is vendor-gated per spec) with the default rule-10 retry semantics (3 attempts, exponential 5s base). Flow: re-check `OrgEhrConnection.writebackEnabled` at pickup (defense in depth; admin may have flipped off between approve + pickup → CANCELLED + `cancelReason: 'worker_recheck'`); mark EXECUTING; dispatch to `createCondition` / `patchCondition`; on success, back-fill `CaseManagement.mirrorsFhirConditionId` in the same `$transaction` as the SUCCEEDED status flip (decision 11 — Sprint-0.16 drift detection works on newly written cases on the next routing run); on failure, write FAILED + categorical `failureKind` + audit; ONLY TRANSIENT throws so BullMQ retries (rule 10 — PERMANENT + CONFLICT fail-closed without burning the retry budget). 10 worker tests in `test/workers/fhir-writeback-handler.test.ts` covering happy-path CREATE + PATCH-status; org-disabled-mid-flight; cancelled-mid-flight; TRANSIENT/PERMANENT/CONFLICT failures; `failureCount` increment; missing FHIR identity → PERMANENT failure path; every terminal state writes its audit row (rule 8 spot-check).
  - **Idempotent state-machine API** — three new routes under `/api/cases/[id]/writeback/`:
    - `approve/route.ts`: PROPOSED → APPROVED + audit + enqueue. Idempotent (already-APPROVED/EXECUTING/SUCCEEDED returns 200 with current status; no second audit, no second enqueue). 409 invalid_state on FAILED/CANCELLED (use /retry or /cancel).
    - `cancel/route.ts`: PROPOSED/FAILED → CANCELLED with `cancelReason: 'clinician'`. 409 on EXECUTING (let the worker finish) and SUCCEEDED (terminal). Idempotent.
    - `retry/route.ts`: FAILED + TRANSIENT → APPROVED + re-enqueue; emits `FHIR_WRITEBACK_APPROVED` with `metadata.retry: true` so the auditor lens can count retry rates. 409 not_retryable on PERMANENT + CONFLICT (must cancel + propose afresh).
    17 API tests across the three routes covering happy paths, idempotency, state-machine 409s, 404s, retry-blocking on permanents.
  - **Accept-endpoint extension** (`/api/notes/[id]/case-router/accept`): new `maybeInsertWriteBackProposal` helper called inside the case-mutation tx. Gates: (1) org `writebackEnabled = true`, (2) action is mutating (`open-new`, `open-new-from-condition`, or `reconcile` with `reopen-case`/`close-case`/`open-new-case`/`update-case-icd`), (3) post-mutation case has a coded ICD; (4) for PATCH paths, the case is mirrored AND the cached `FhirCachedResource` carries a `meta.versionId` (`If-Match` mandatory — decision 6). Inserts the row at `PROPOSED` + emits `FHIR_WRITEBACK_PROPOSED` INSIDE the tx. Response gains optional `writeBackProposal: { id, operation, summary }` field — UI uses presence (not the toggle) to render the inline "Write to EHR?" section so non-eligible / writeback-off paths see identical Sprint-0.16 behavior. attach / attach-with-secondary / attach-as-is never write back (decisions 8 + 9). 4 new accept-endpoint tests (16 → 16 total): writeback-enabled open-new inserts the proposal + audit; writeback-disabled is byte-identical to Sprint 0.16 (no proposal, no audit, no enqueue); attach + writeback-enabled gates out at the trigger stage (no orgEhrConnection lookup); reconcile + attach-as-is + writeback-enabled returns null proposal.
  - **Review-panel UI** (`src/app/(clinical)/review/[noteId]/_components/case-routing-panel.tsx`): new `WriteBackInlineSection` rendered alongside the existing `AcceptedPill` when the accept response carries a non-null `writeBackProposal`. Three states: not-decided (shows summary + "Yes, write to EHR" / "Not now" pair), dialog-open (`<WriteBackConfirmDialog>` with the FHIR Condition payload + ICD + status + recorder display + a Confirm button), approved (small "EHR write queued" `<StatusBadge variant="info">`). Both `ProposalCard.confirm` and `ReconcileCard.confirm` parse the accept response's `writeBackProposal` field and bubble it up via the `onResolved` callback (signature `(writeBack | null) => void`); the parent's `CaseRoutingPanel` holds the state. `ManualPicker` (attach-only path) calls `onResolved(null)` since attach is never write-back-eligible.
  - **Confirmation dialog** (`src/components/fhir/writeback-confirm-dialog.tsx`): `<AlertDialog>` (rule 22 — not native `confirm()`). Renders the summary + an optional grid of structured detail rows + the PHI-free expectation copy ("review the result in your EHR after the write completes"). Confirm POSTs to `/api/cases/{caseId}/writeback/approve`. On success the host flips to "queued"; on failure the inline `<StatusBanner variant="danger">` surfaces the message.
  - **Cases-panel chip** (`src/components/fhir/writeback-status-chip.tsx` + `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/_components/cases-panel.tsx` + `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/page.tsx`): per-row `<StatusBadge>` driven by the most-recent non-terminal `FhirWriteBackProposal` for each case. Variants per spec: PROPOSED → neutral "EHR sync pending"; APPROVED/EXECUTING → info "EHR write queued"; FAILED + TRANSIENT → warning "EHR write failed — retry" (clickable); FAILED + PERMANENT/CONFLICT → danger "EHR write blocked — review" (clickable to drawer). SUCCEEDED / CANCELLED render nothing (terminal-silent). Server-side query pulls one proposal per case via `take: 1` ordered by `proposedAt desc`.
  - **Org-settings master toggle** (`src/app/(admin)/settings/ehr/_components/writeback-toggle.tsx` + `src/app/api/admin/org-settings/ehr-writeback-toggle/route.ts`): `<Switch>` card that defaults FALSE for every existing org. Enable: stamps `writebackEnabledAt`/`writebackEnabledByUserId` + `ORG_EHR_WRITEBACK_ENABLED` audit. Disable: clears the timestamp + `ORG_EHR_WRITEBACK_DISABLED` audit + batch-cancels every PROPOSED/APPROVED proposal for the org (atomic `$transaction` for the flag + the `updateMany`) + emits a per-row `FHIR_WRITEBACK_CANCELLED` audit with `cancelReason: 'org_disabled'`. The worker's pickup-time re-check uses the same `cancelReason: 'worker_recheck'` discriminator so the auditor lens distinguishes batched (admin) and per-job (worker) cancellation cohorts.
  - **Audit (7 new actions)** — `FHIR_WRITEBACK_PROPOSED`, `_APPROVED`, `_SUCCEEDED`, `_FAILED`, `_CANCELLED` (clinician cohort, all `personaVersion: 'miss-cleo-v1'`); `ORG_EHR_WRITEBACK_ENABLED`, `_DISABLED` (admin cohort, with `cancelledProposalCount` on disable). All PHI-free — `fhirConditionId` + `resultFhirId` are EHR-side identifiers, `failureKind` is categorical, `failureMessage` stays on the row (not in audit metadata). Five-row chain per successful write: PROPOSED → APPROVED → SUCCEEDED (+ optional CANCELLED if the user later cancels; or → FAILED → APPROVED-retry on transients).
  - **Backward compatibility (decision 10 — verified)**: with `writebackEnabled = false` (every existing org's default), the accept endpoint is BYTE-IDENTICAL to Sprint 0.16 — zero proposal rows, zero `FHIR_WRITEBACK_*` audits, zero worker jobs enqueued, no inline UI section rendered, no chip on cases-panel. Verified by the dedicated "writebackEnabled=false → no proposal, no FHIR_WRITEBACK_* audit" test (and by all 12 pre-Sprint-0.17 accept tests still passing unchanged with `writebackOffDefaults()` injected into their tx mocks).
  - **Files** (new): `prisma/migrations/20260524000000_sprint_0_17_fhir_writeback/migration.sql`; `src/services/fhir/case-writeback.ts`; `src/workers/fhir-writeback/handler.ts`; `src/workers/fhir-writeback.worker.ts`; `src/app/api/cases/[id]/writeback/{approve,cancel,retry}/route.ts`; `src/app/api/admin/org-settings/ehr-writeback-toggle/route.ts`; `src/components/fhir/writeback-status-chip.tsx`; `src/components/fhir/writeback-confirm-dialog.tsx`; `src/app/(admin)/settings/ehr/_components/writeback-toggle.tsx`; `test/services/fhir/case-writeback.test.ts`; `test/workers/fhir-writeback-handler.test.ts`; `test/api/case-writeback-{approve,cancel,retry}.test.ts`.
  - **Files** (modified): `prisma/schema.prisma`; `package.json` + `package-lock.json` (added `@paralleldrive/cuid2` for the `idempotencyKey` generator); `src/services/fhir/patient-client.ts`; `src/lib/queue.ts`; `src/workers/index.ts`; `src/lib/audit/actions.ts`; `src/app/api/notes/[id]/case-router/accept/route.ts`; `src/app/(clinical)/review/[noteId]/_components/case-routing-panel.tsx`; `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/_components/cases-panel.tsx`; `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/page.tsx`; `test/api/case-router-accept.test.ts`.
  - **Verify**: `npm run typecheck` clean; `npx eslint <touched files>` clean; `REDIS_URL="" DATABASE_URL="" npx vitest run` → 768 tests in 74 files (was 707 baseline + 30 service + 10 worker + 17 API + 4 accept = 61 net; 12 integration files still skipping cleanly under the unset-env mirror of CI); `npx prisma generate` + `npx prisma db seed` clean.
  - **Three-lens**: **Clinician** — write-back is a *help*, not a *task*. One explicit click after confirming the case action, one confirmation modal with the payload, and Cleo handles the rest. When the write fails, the OS-side workflow is unaffected — the clinician can finish the visit, sign the note, and decide later whether to retry from the chart. The cases-panel surfaces status without becoming a todo list (SUCCEEDED is terminal-silent). **Compliance** — every write-back is a five-row audit trail (PROPOSED → APPROVED → SUCCEEDED or FAILED; + optional CANCELLED). The `omniscribe-origin` extension on the FHIR resource lets an external auditor identify which Conditions originated in OmniScribe versus the EHR's native pathway. One join reconstructs "who wrote what to which EHR resource, and when." **Auditor** — failure taxonomy is preserved end-to-end: TRANSIENT failures are retryable and don't pollute the permanent-failure cohort; PERMANENT and CONFLICT failures surface as distinct categorical signals so an org-admin querying "which writes need attention" gets a precise list. The `idempotencyKey` + `If-Match` pattern means we can prove no double-write under worker retry — the EHR-side resource history shows one POST or one PATCH per proposal.
  - **Out of scope** (deferred): bulk back-fill of OS-only legacy cases; MedicationStatement / AllergyIntolerance write-back; EHR-side webhook receiver; patient demographic sync; vendor-specific PUT fallback for Conditions (we always send JSON Patch; the spec calls out the PUT fallback option as available but not required this sprint).

- **2026-05-22 — Sprint 0.16: FHIR Phase D₂ — Case ↔ Condition reconciliation** (`feat(sprint-0.16): fhir-reconciliation`).
  - **Spec**: `context/specs/sprint-0-fhir-reconciliation.md`. Builds additively on Sprint 0.15 (FHIR Phase D₁ populated `mirrorsFhirConditionId`).
  - **Schema migration** — `prisma/migrations/20260523120000_sprint_0_16_fhir_reconciliation`. Additive only: new `CaseFhirDriftLog` model (one row per detected drift; snapshots both sides + carries `resolvedAt`/`resolvedAction`/`resolvedByUserId`) + new `CaseFhirDriftKind` enum (`STATUS`, `ICD`; append-only thereafter). No existing column or enum changes. `npx prisma db seed` clean (rule 4).
  - **Drift detector — pure function** (`src/services/copilot/case-router-fhir.ts`): `detectDriftSignals(cases, conditions)` — deterministic, no side effects, no DB or LLM. Implements the full spec decision-table (ACTIVE × resolved/remission → STATUS drift; CLOSED × active/recurrence/relapse → STATUS drift; CANCELLED / PENDING_ROUTER → skip; ICD drift when both ICDs coded + differ). Exhaustive unit tests: 31 cases in `test/services/copilot/case-router-drift-detection.test.ts` covering every row of the table + ICD-drift rule + corner cases (no mirror, missing condition, idempotency, recorder provenance carries through).
  - **Mirrored-Condition fetcher**: same file adds `fetchMirroredConditions(orgId, patientId, fhirConditionIds)` — fetches cached Conditions by id WITHOUT the active-only filter Sprint 0.15's `fetchPatientConditions` applies. Rule 20 gates preserved (verified `PatientFhirIdentity`, cached resources only, no live HTTP). `FhirConditionForRouter.clinicalStatus` widened to the full FHIR-R4 union so the drift detector can see non-active values.
  - **Agent extension** (`src/services/copilot/case-router.ts`): `CaseRouterProposalSchema` gains `'reconcile'` action + `reconcileProposal` payload (`driftLogId`, `caseManagementId`, `fhirConditionId`, `driftKind`, `summary`, `resolutionOptions` (min 2, max 4) with `kind ∈ { reopen-case | open-new-case | close-case | attach-as-is | update-case-icd }`, optional `recommendedOptionIndex`). New `CaseRouterInput.driftSignals` optional field. New drift-handling system-prompt block gated on the `driftAware` flag — only appended when `driftSignals.length > 0`. `validateProposalAgainstInput` rejects hallucinated `driftLogId` / `caseManagementId` references; coerces `confidence === 'high'` down to `'medium'` per spec decision 7 (system detected the drift, clinician resolves — confidence bounded).
  - **Worker wiring** (`src/workers/case-router/handler.ts`): after the FHIR active fetch, if (a) FHIR enabled at org, (b) the active fetch did NOT degrade, and (c) any case carries `mirrorsFhirConditionId`, calls `fetchMirroredConditions` → `detectDriftSignals` → pre-persists a `CaseFhirDriftLog` row per signal → emits `CASE_FHIR_DRIFT_DETECTED` per signal (rule 8 — never swallowed) → threads `driftSignals` into the agent input. After the run persists, back-fills `detectedByRunId` via `updateMany`. If the agent's proposal carries `action: 'reconcile'`, emits `CASE_ROUTER_RECONCILE_PROPOSED` with `driftLogId` + `optionsCount` + persona version.
  - **Accept endpoint** (`/api/notes/[id]/case-router/accept`): new `reconcile` decision kind with discriminated `resolution` payload (`reopen-case` / `attach-as-is` / `close-case` (with optional `reason`) / `open-new-case` / `update-case-icd`). Per-kind transaction handlers execute the case mutation atomically with the drift-log resolution (`resolvedAt` / `resolvedAction` / `resolvedByUserId`) AND emit `CASE_FHIR_DRIFT_RESOLVED` inside the same tx — a throw rolls all three back together. `ReconcileAlreadyResolvedError` thrown when another reviewer beat us to it → 409 `drift_already_resolved`.
  - **Review-panel UI** (`case-routing-panel.tsx`): when `proposal.action === 'reconcile'`, the parent dispatches to `ReconcileCard` (not `ProposalCard`) so hooks fire unconditionally (react-hooks rules). ReconcileCard renders the amber drift banner (`StatusBanner variant="warning"`) with the agent `summary`, the 2-4 resolution radios with reasoning subtitles, and pre-selects `recommendedOptionIndex` when set. Confirm posts `{ kind: 'reconcile', driftLogId, resolution: {...} }`. The standard alternatives + "Change manually" fallback are deliberately absent from the reconcile path (decision 6 — reconcile REPLACES attach at the top level).
  - **Reusable amber banner**: new `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/_components/case-fhir-drift-banner.tsx` — `StatusBanner variant="warning"` + `AlertTriangle` icon + the summary + a drift-kind chip. Used by the reconcile card now; Sprint 0.18's chart tab will reuse it for unresolved drifts.
  - **State-builder integration** (`src/services/copilot/state-builder.ts`): `ObservedPatternBaseSchema.kind` gains `'case_fhir_status_drift'`. New pure `detectCaseFhirDrift(driftLogs)` exported. `buildStateProjections` loads `caseFhirDriftLog` rows where `resolvedAt: null` for the patient. `CLEO_STATE_GENERATOR_VERSION` bumped to `'cleo-state-v3'` so existing rows refresh on next event.
  - **Audit (3 new actions appended)** — `CASE_FHIR_DRIFT_DETECTED`, `CASE_ROUTER_RECONCILE_PROPOSED`, `CASE_FHIR_DRIFT_RESOLVED`. All PHI-free metadata; all carry `personaVersion: 'miss-cleo-v1'` (Sprint 0.12 lineage).
  - **Backward compatibility (decision 10 — verified)**: a non-mirrored case → drift detection short-circuits + NO log rows + agent prompt is byte-identical to Sprint 0.15. FHIR-unhealthy run (active fetch returned `_FHIR_UNAVAILABLE`) → drift detection is also skipped → no log rows, no reconcile proposal. Both paths covered by dedicated worker tests.
  - **Files** (new): `prisma/migrations/20260523120000_sprint_0_16_fhir_reconciliation/migration.sql`; `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/_components/case-fhir-drift-banner.tsx`; `test/services/copilot/case-router-drift-detection.test.ts`.
  - **Files** (modified): `prisma/schema.prisma`; `src/lib/audit/actions.ts`; `src/services/copilot/{case-router,case-router-fhir,state-builder}.ts`; `src/workers/case-router/handler.ts`; `src/app/api/notes/[id]/case-router/accept/route.ts`; `src/app/(clinical)/review/[noteId]/_components/case-routing-panel.tsx`; 4 test files extended.
  - **Verify**: `npm run lint` — clean on all sprint-touched files; `npm run typecheck` — clean; `npm test` — 707 / 707 (was 658 baseline + 31 drift-detector + 4 worker + 8 agent + 4 accept + 4 panel = +49 new — over-counts a couple of helper renames that absorbed pre-existing scenarios, but net is 707); `npx prisma db seed` — clean.
  - **Three-lens**: Clinician — the system catches the EHR-vs-OmniScribe drift the clinician would otherwise miss, surfaces the *what* + the *when*, offers explicit clinical paths, and never makes the call. One tap with the right framing. Compliance — every drift event is recorded in `CaseFhirDriftLog` with snapshots of both sides at detection time + the clinician's resolution alongside. Future audits reconstruct *"why did this case close on this date?"* with one join — drift detected, resolution chosen, mutation applied. Auditor — `CASE_FHIR_DRIFT_DETECTED` distinguishes *"system saw the drift"* from `CASE_FHIR_DRIFT_RESOLVED` *"clinician resolved it on a specific note's review."* Open drifts (detected but unresolved) become a queryable cohort for org-level data-quality monitoring.

- **2026-05-22 — Sprint 0.15: FHIR Phase D₁ — Conditions in Miss Cleo's case-router** (`feat(sprint-0.15): fhir-case-router`).
  - **Spec**: `context/specs/sprint-0-fhir-case-router.md`. Builds additively on Sprint 0.13 (case-router agent) + Sprint 0.14 (persistent memory + `caseAwarenessJson`). Pure code change — no schema migration, no new worker.
  - **What shipped — additive FHIR routing path**:
    1. **`src/lib/case-management/fhir-router-config.ts`** — org-level gate `isFhirRouterEnabled(orgId)` returns true iff `OrgEhrConnection.enabled` exists. Used by the case-router worker AND the existing dedup endpoint so both Cleo's agentic path and the manual `NewCaseDialog` fallback share one source of truth (decision 8).
    2. **`src/services/copilot/case-router-fhir.ts`** — pure fetcher + citation projector. Reads cached `FhirCachedResource` rows (rule 20: the cache is populated EXCLUSIVELY from verified `PatientFhirIdentity` links via the F3 sync — the canonical "verified FHIR" path; no live HTTP calls inside the worker). Returns `{ok:true, conditions[]}` for the happy path or `{ok:false, errorKind: 'not_linked' | 'no_cache' | 'timeout' | 'cache_error'}` on degradation. 4s wall-clock bound; never throws (rule 10 — BullMQ retries reserved for genuine agent / DB failures).
    3. **Agent extension (`src/services/copilot/case-router.ts`)** — `CaseRouterProposalSchema` grows by one action `'open-new-from-condition'` + `newCaseFromCondition` payload (required `primaryIcd` — the whole point is a verified coded value) + `fhirCitations` array. New optional `CaseRouterInput.fhirConditions` field. `buildCaseRouterSystemPrompt({fhirAware: true})` appends a FHIR-citation guidance block; `buildCaseRouterUserMessage` emits a `<fhir_conditions>` block. Validation rejects hallucinated `fhirConditionId` values (filters alternatives, fails closed on primary). Sprint-0.13 / 0.14 prompts are byte-identical when `fhirConditions` is absent (decision 10).
    4. **Worker wiring (`src/workers/case-router/handler.ts`)** — calls `isFhirRouterEnabled` then `fetchPatientConditions`; threads conditions into the agent input; stamps `fhirCitations` onto the persisted `proposalJson`; emits `CASE_ROUTER_FHIR_CITED` when at least one citation lands; emits `CASE_ROUTER_FHIR_UNAVAILABLE` for `no_cache` / `timeout` / `cache_error` (NOT for `not_linked` — that's the baseline state, not a degradation). `fhirConditionInputCount` added to `CASE_ROUTER_PROPOSED` metadata for the auditor lens.
    5. **Accept endpoint (`/api/notes/[id]/case-router/accept`)** — new `open-new-from-condition` branch promotes the pending case (or creates + rebinds if the encounter already ran past `PENDING_ROUTER`) with the coded `primaryIcd` + `mirrorsFhirConditionId`. Emits `CASE_FHIR_LINKED` inside the same tx so rollback covers the data + audit pair.
    6. **Review-panel UI (`case-routing-panel.tsx`)** — adds the fourth action rendering. The radio carries an EHR-verified `StatusBadge` (success variant + `BadgeCheck` icon) plus a citation line *"✓ EHR-verified · recorded YYYY-MM-DD by \<recorder\>"*. The pill is conditional on `choice.fhirCitation` so plain `open-new` retains its "Needs coding" semantics. HIGH-confidence on the FHIR-backed action pre-selects it (decision 5 — option 0 is already the default selection for HIGH).
    7. **State-builder (`src/services/copilot/state-builder.ts`)** — populates `caseAwarenessJson[].fhirMirror` for every case with `mirrorsFhirConditionId`; reads the matching `FhirCachedResource` to fill `clinicalStatus` + `lastUpdated`. Schema extended with the new fields. `CLEO_STATE_GENERATOR_VERSION` bumped to `cleo-state-v2` so existing rows refresh on the next event.
    8. **Dedup endpoint (`/api/case-management/check-dups`)** — now returns `fhirConditions[]` alongside `existingCases[]` (decision 8); each Condition carries a `mirroredByCaseId` cross-reference so a future dialog UI can mark already-mirrored Conditions. Same FHIR fetcher; same graceful degradation.
  - **Audit (3 new actions)** — `CASE_ROUTER_FHIR_CITED` (per cited run; `{caseRouterRunId, citationCount, fhirIds[], ehrSystem, personaVersion}`); `CASE_FHIR_LINKED` (per case opened from a Condition; `{caseManagementId, caseRouterRunId, fhirConditionId, personaVersion}`); `CASE_ROUTER_FHIR_UNAVAILABLE` (per degraded fetch; `{caseRouterRunId, patientId, errorKind, personaVersion}`). All PHI-free — `fhirId` is an EHR-side identifier, never HIPAA Safe Harbor PHI.
  - **Backward compatibility (decision 10 — verified)**: every test path that doesn't supply `fhirConditions` runs byte-identical to Sprint 0.14: same prompt, same Zod schema acceptance, same audit shape (just `+fhirConditionInputCount: 0`). The worker test suite default-mocks `OrgEhrConnection.count = 0` so the existing 5 Sprint-0.13/0.14 scenarios are unaffected. The `not_linked` audit suppression confirmed in a dedicated test — non-FHIR-linked patient on a FHIR-enabled org emits zero FHIR audits.
  - **Files** (new): `src/lib/case-management/fhir-router-config.ts`; `src/services/copilot/case-router-fhir.ts`; `test/services/copilot/case-router-fhir.test.ts`; `test/components/case-routing-panel.test.tsx`.
  - **Files** (modified): `src/services/copilot/{case-router,state-builder}.ts`; `src/workers/case-router/handler.ts`; `src/app/api/notes/[id]/case-router/accept/route.ts`; `src/app/api/case-management/check-dups/route.ts`; `src/app/(clinical)/review/[noteId]/_components/case-routing-panel.tsx`; `src/lib/audit/actions.ts`; `test/workers/case-router-handler.test.ts`; `test/api/case-router-accept.test.ts`; `test/lib/case-router/propose.test.ts`.
  - **Verify**: `npm run typecheck` clean; `npm test` 658/658 (was 633 baseline + 4 fetcher + 3 worker + 1 accept + 4 agent + 3 panel = 15 new + 10 backward-compat reaffirmations); ESLint clean on all 14 touched files; `npx prisma db seed` clean (no schema change).
  - **Three-lens**: Clinician — when the EHR has the diagnosis coded already, Miss Cleo proposes it back with verified provenance; one tap to confirm; no manual ICD entry, no "Needs coding" badge. When the EHR is silent or the patient isn't linked, behavior is identical to yesterday — zero regression. Compliance — every FHIR-cited routing decision is captured end-to-end: `Condition.fhirId` + `recordedDate` + `recorder` are persisted in `CaseRouterRun.proposalJson.fhirCitations`, audited via `CASE_ROUTER_FHIR_CITED`, and linked to the resulting case via `mirrorsFhirConditionId` + `CASE_FHIR_LINKED`. Single coherent provenance chain. Auditor — `CASE_ROUTER_FHIR_UNAVAILABLE` is recorded explicitly when the system degraded — never a silent fall-through. The trail distinguishes *"the agent never had FHIR data"* (no audit, non-linked baseline) from *"the agent had FHIR enabled, tried, and the cache failed"* (`errorKind` audit row).

- **2026-05-22 — Sprint 0.14: Miss Cleo's persistent memory + "Cleo's read" chart card** (`feat(sprint-0.14): cleo-persistent-memory`).
  - **Spec**: `context/specs/sprint-0-cleo-persistent-memory.md`. Builds on Sprint 0.13 (case-router) for the prior-cross-visit context wiring + on Sprint 0.12 (persona pass) for `personaVersion` audit cohort filtering.
  - **What shipped (Phase A — schema + projection)**:
    1. **Schema (additive only)** — three new models + one enum, no changes to existing tables. `CopilotPatientState` (per `org × patient × clinician` projection cache; `caseAwarenessJson` + `observedPatternsJson` + `conversationFactsJson` + `generatorVersion`). `CopilotConversation` (one persistent thread per `org × patient × clinician × mode`; research-mode rows are `patientId = null` with a partial-unique singleton index per `org × clinician`). `CopilotMessage` (append-only, role + content + sourcesJson + toolCallsJson; cascade delete from conversation). `CopilotConversationMode` enum (`CHART` | `RESEARCH`). Migration `20260523000000_sprint_0_14_cleo_persistent_memory` — fully additive, `npx prisma db seed` clean (rule 4).
    2. **`src/services/copilot/state-builder.ts`** — pure projection rebuilder. Reads ONLY rule-20 sources: `Note.status IN (SIGNED, TRANSFERRED)`, `CaseManagement`, `CaseRouterRun`, `FollowUp`, `EpisodeOfCare` + goals + progress entries, `NoteBrief.content`. Zod-validated output. Idempotent + deterministic — no LLM calls. Four pattern detectors per spec catalog: `topic_mentioned_unaddressed` (keyword scan over last N transcripts vs. plan), `measure_trend` (monotonic over ≥3 readings from `NoteBrief.objectiveMeasures`), `recert_due_soon` (REHAB `recertDueAt` within 14 days), `goal_stalled` (ACTIVE goal with no `GoalProgressEntry` in 28+ days). Bumpable `generatorVersion` ('cleo-state-v1') so future shape changes re-trigger rebuilds.
    3. **`src/lib/case-management/viewer-recency.ts`** — shared three-tier recency helper extracted per spec; the patient-chart page + the state-builder compute the same `viewerLastActivityAt` / `viewerDivisionLastActivityAt` / `lastActivityAt` so the chart hero pick and Cleo's memory agree on what "yours" means.
    4. **`src/workers/cleo-state/handler.ts`** + new `cleo-state` BullMQ queue. Throttle: stable per-tuple jobId per 5-minute bucket coalesces burst events (decision 5). Standard retry policy (3 attempts / exponential backoff — rule 10). Audits `CLEO_STATE_REBUILT` with PHI-free metadata (`{stateId, patientId, clinicianOrgUserId, generatorVersion, rebuildDurationMs, patternCount, caseCount, factCount, personaVersion}`) — never wrapped in swallowing try-catch (rule 8). Defense-in-depth org-scope check rejects cross-org clinician ids.
    5. **Chain-enqueue from three sites**:
        - `src/workers/ai-generation/handler.ts` — both completion paths fire `enqueueCleoStateRefresh` for the note's authoring clinician (alongside the existing `enqueueCaseRouterJob`).
        - `src/app/api/notes/[id]/sign/route.ts` — on sign, enqueues for the signing clinician AND fans out to every other clinician with an existing `CopilotPatientState` row on the patient (so peers learn from the new sign too).
        - `src/app/api/notes/[id]/case-router/accept/route.ts` — on acceptance, enqueues for the accepting clinician (the new routing decision is a primary signal Cleo's state should reflect).
  - **What shipped (Phase B — conversation persistence + case-router wiring)**:
    1. **`src/services/copilot/conversation-store.ts`** — pure helper layer for `loadOrCreateConversation` / `appendTurn` / `purgeConversation`. Encodes the "OPENED audit fires once" + "history loaded from DB" + "two-write transaction" disciplines so both `/api/copilot/ask` and `/api/copilot/research` use the same patterns. Race-safe creation on the compound unique key.
    2. **`/api/copilot/ask`** — now loads/creates a `CopilotConversation` per call, hydrates the agent's prompt context from the DB-stored history (no more client-shipped `history`), persists both the user message + assistant response in a transaction. Audits `CLEO_CONVERSATION_OPENED` once when the row is created. Response includes `conversationId` so the surface can drive the reset action.
    3. **`/api/copilot/research`** — same treatment for research-mode threads. One thread per `(org × clinician)` patient-agnostic; partial-unique index in the migration enforces singleton.
    4. **`/api/copilot/conversations` (GET) + `/api/copilot/conversations/[id]` (DELETE)** — hydration endpoint for surface mount; reset endpoint that purges the conversation + cascades to messages. `CLEO_CONVERSATION_PURGED` audit carries the message count + persona version. The `CopilotPatientState` row is NOT touched (decision 9 — chat thread reset is distinct from memory wipe).
    5. **`AskSurface` + `ResearchSurface`** — hydrate persisted messages on mount. First-open greeting bubble now only fires for *truly* brand-new conversations (post-hydration, zero messages). New header strip surfaces "Conversation saved with this patient." + a Reset menu item gated by an `<AlertDialog>` (rule 22; no native confirm). Returning conversations pick up where the clinician left off — no greeting.
    6. **Case-router wiring (Sprint 0.13 extension, backward-compatible)** — `src/services/copilot/case-router.ts` exposes `buildPriorCrossVisitContextBlock(state)` + accepts an optional `priorCrossVisitContext` string on `CaseRouterInput`. The case-router worker reads `CopilotPatientState` if present, builds the block, threads it through to `propose()`. State-absent path runs identically to Sprint 0.13. The audit `CASE_ROUTER_PROPOSED` metadata gains a `hadPriorCrossVisitContext: boolean` for the auditor lens.
  - **What shipped (Phase C — UI)**:
    1. **`src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/_components/cleo-read-card.tsx`** — the "✨ Cleo's read" 30-second answer surface. Renders the headline stat strip (active cases + open follow-ups + "Your active case" pill), up to 4 pattern labels with a "Patterns noted (N)" header, and an "Ask me anything" CTA. Empty-state path (no state row yet) shows the "I'm just learning this patient — open the Ask sheet to get started." stub per decision 7.
    2. **Server-side projection in `patients/[id]/page.tsx`** — fetches `CopilotPatientState` for the viewing clinician + maps the JSON shapes into a card-friendly `CleoReadCardData` (PHI-fenced: forwards labels + counts only; detector `detail` bodies stay server-side).
    3. **`patient-chart-tabs.tsx`** mounts the card at the TOP of the Overview tab (above the existing SnapshotInlineStrip + cockpit tiles per decision 6). The CTA dispatches a global `cleo:open-sheet` event; `CopilotShell` listens for it and opens the Sheet — lightest-touch coupling between two always-mounted shells without a parent prop drill.
  - **Audit (3 new actions)**:
    - `CLEO_STATE_REBUILT` — worker upserts a state row. Metadata: `{stateId, patientId, clinicianOrgUserId, generatorVersion, rebuildDurationMs, patternCount, caseCount, factCount, personaVersion}`.
    - `CLEO_CONVERSATION_OPENED` — first message in a fresh conversation row. Metadata: `{conversationId, mode, patientId, personaVersion}` (patientId null for RESEARCH).
    - `CLEO_CONVERSATION_PURGED` — "Reset this conversation" fires. Metadata: `{conversationId, mode, patientId, messageCount, personaVersion}`.
  - **Tests** (34 new — all pass; total 633/633):
    - `test/services/copilot/state-builder.test.ts` (15) — each pattern detector fires correctly + skip cases, idempotency, Zod schema acceptance for all three projection shapes.
    - `test/api/copilot-ask-conversation-persistence.test.ts` (2) — first message creates conversation + audits OPENED with persona; subsequent messages reuse it + thread DB history into the agent input.
    - `test/workers/cleo-state-handler.test.ts` (5) — happy path with PHI-free metadata, cross-org clinician rejection, missing clinician, upsert retry rethrow, jobId-bucket throttle smoke test.
    - `test/components/cleo-read-card.test.tsx` (5) — populated card renders headline + patterns + CTA, CTA invokes onAskOpen, pattern list capped at 4 with total count, hidden CTA when no callback, empty-state path + CTA.
    - `test/workers/case-router-handler.test.ts` updated to mock `copilotPatientState.findUnique` (state-absent default keeps Sprint 0.13 backward-compatibility assertions intact).
  - **Files** (new): migration; `src/services/copilot/{state-builder,conversation-store}.ts`; `src/lib/case-management/viewer-recency.ts`; `src/workers/{cleo-state.worker.ts,cleo-state/handler.ts}`; `src/app/api/copilot/conversations/{route.ts,[id]/route.ts}`; `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/_components/cleo-read-card.tsx`; 4 new test files.
  - **Files** (modified): `prisma/schema.prisma` (3 new models + enum + relations on Organization/User/Patient); `src/lib/{audit/actions.ts,queue.ts}`; `src/workers/{index.ts,ai-generation/handler.ts,case-router/handler.ts}`; `src/services/copilot/case-router.ts` (priorCrossVisitContext field + block builder); `src/app/api/copilot/{ask,research}/route.ts`; `src/app/api/notes/[id]/{sign,case-router/accept}/route.ts`; `src/components/copilot/{ask-surface,research-surface,copilot-shell}.tsx`; `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/{page.tsx,_components/patient-chart-tabs.tsx}`; `test/workers/case-router-handler.test.ts`.
  - **Locked decisions applied**: per-(patient × clinician) scoping; state is a projection from primary sources; one persistent thread per tuple × mode; PHI in messages under the same at-rest posture as note bodies; event-driven refresh (no polling); card at top of Overview; fresh-clinician empty-state with lazy build; `generatorVersion` bump signal; conversation reset doesn't purge memory; out-of-scope items (cross-clinician sharing, LLM summarization, proactive nudges, FHIR Conditions, retention config, export) explicitly deferred.
  - **Verify**: `npm run typecheck` clean; `npm test` 633/633 (was 599 + 34 new); ESLint clean on all 29 touched files (per `ReadLints`); `npx prisma db seed` clean.
  - **Three-lens**: Clinician — Miss Cleo becomes a colleague who remembers; open the chart → see her current read; open the Sheet → pick up the conversation where it was; the case-router gets better silently as she learns the patient. Compliance — every persistent surface (state row, conversation, message) carries `personaVersion`; the state projection is rebuildable from primary sources, so it's never a divergence risk — truth still lives in signed notes, cases, follow-ups, FHIR; PHI in messages stored under the same at-rest discipline as note bodies. Auditor — `CLEO_STATE_REBUILT` traces what Cleo knew when; the conversation history reconstructs every clinician-AI exchange; combined with `CASE_ROUTER_PROPOSED/ACCEPTED` (Sprint 0.13) and `COPILOT_ASK_ANSWERED` (existing), one query answers *"what did Cleo know + do for this patient with this clinician?"*.

- **2026-05-22 — Sprint 0.13: Miss Cleo's case-router agent (Phase A + B)** (`feat(sprint-0.13): case-router-agent`).
  - **Spec**: `context/specs/sprint-0-case-router-agent.md`. Builds on Sprint 0.11 (case management) + 0.12 (persona pass) — both shipped first.
  - **What shipped (Phase A)**:
    1. **Schema (additive)** — `PENDING_ROUTER` appended to `CaseManagementStatus` (rule 2). New `CaseRouterRun` model + `RouterConfidence` enum (HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW). New nullable `mirrorsFhirConditionId` column on `CaseManagement` (forward-compatible with Sprint 0.15 FHIR phase). Migration `20260522180000_sprint_0_13_case_router` — fully additive, idempotent, no backfill.
    2. **Encounter flow** — `src/lib/encounters/start.ts` accepts an OPTIONAL `caseManagementId`. When omitted, the server auto-creates a `PENDING_ROUTER` case inside the same transaction and binds the encounter to it. `assertCaseIsOpen` now allows both `ACTIVE` and `PENDING_ROUTER`. `resolveCaseManagementIdForVisit` returns `null` instead of throwing `case_required` so `startVisit` is the single owner of the auto-create step. The four caller routes (`/api/encounters`, `/api/schedules/[id]/start`, `/api/admin/telehealth/sessions/[id]/start`) thread the optional id through.
    3. **`StartVisitDialog` default flow** — auto-posts WITHOUT a case id (`source: 'auto-none'`); the case picker becomes the OVERRIDE path. New `forceCaseId` prop set by the chart hero "Continue this case" button binds explicitly. The picker only renders when forced (site picker, late-entry path, or REHAB clinician with 2+ episodes on a forced case).
  - **What shipped (Phase B)**:
    1. **`src/services/copilot/case-router.ts`** — the agent service. Single-shot LLM call (no tool loop; bounded inputs). Zod-validated `CaseRouterProposalSchema` (`attach` / `attach-with-secondary` / `open-new` actions; `confidence` HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW; up to 3 `alternatives`). System prompt prefixes `buildPersonaSystemBlock('chart')` + `PERSONA_ANTI_DRIFT_BLOCK` (rule 24 enforced in copy: "data routing only — never clinical recommendations"). Stub-mode awareness: synthetic LOW-confidence `open-new` proposal so the panel always renders. Fallback path covers Sonnet→Haiku failover + parse failure + hallucinated case id. Decision is single-shot; reasoning rule cites case ids or Assessment fragments — never speculates.
    2. **`src/workers/case-router/handler.ts`** — BullMQ worker. Listens on a new `case-router` queue with the standard 3-retry exponential backoff (rule 10). Loads the note + clinician profession + open cases (excluding the encounter's PENDING_ROUTER row). Calls `CaseRouterService.propose()`. Upserts `CaseRouterRun` (idempotent on noteId). Audits `CASE_ROUTER_PROPOSED` with PHI-free metadata (`{caseRouterRunId, confidence, modelVersion, action, alternativesCount, stub, personaVersion}`). Throws on agent failure so BullMQ retries; the catch records an `agent_threw` audit row first (rule 8 — never swallowed).
    3. **Chain-enqueue** — `src/workers/ai-generation/handler.ts` calls `enqueueCaseRouterJob` at both `NOTE_GENERATION_COMPLETED` paths (no-transcript shortcut + main loop). Same pattern as `enqueueNoteBriefJob` from the sign route. Idempotent on noteId.
    4. **`POST /api/notes/[id]/case-router/accept`** — atomic `attach` / `attach-with-secondary` / `open-new` resolution. `attach` rebinds the encounter + deletes the source PENDING_ROUTER case. `attach-with-secondary` adds the new ICD only when the slot is empty. `open-new` promotes the pending case in-place when bound to one (preserves the encounter's case id; idempotent). Decision-vs-proposal diff drives audit action: `CASE_ROUTER_ACCEPTED` when matching, `CASE_ROUTER_OVERRIDDEN` otherwise. Authorization: `requireFeatureAccess('NOTE_EDIT')` + author OR `ORG_ADMIN`. Refuses on SIGNED notes (routing locked at sign).
    5. **`GET /api/notes/[id]/case-router`** — returns the latest `CaseRouterRun` + the patient's open cases (excluding the encounter's currently-bound case). The review-screen panel polls this when the worker hasn't fired yet.
    6. **`/review/[noteId]` panel (`case-routing-panel.tsx`)** — mounted above the section accordions. Server-renders the `CaseRouterRun` when the worker fired before page load; polls every 5s for up to 60s otherwise (then falls through to a manual-pick fallback). Confidence-gated UI (HIGH = pre-select + loud Confirm CTA; MEDIUM = pre-select + Why expanded; LOW = no pre-selection). "Change manually…" branch reuses the picker pattern; collapses to a green checkmark pill after acceptance.
    7. **Audit** — three new actions appended (`CASE_ROUTER_PROPOSED` / `_ACCEPTED` / `_OVERRIDDEN`). Every metadata blob carries `personaVersion: 'miss-cleo-v1'`. PHI fence: structural counts + enums only; reasoning + ICD codes live on `CaseRouterRun`, not in metadata.
    8. **Tests** — `test/lib/case-router/propose.test.ts` (14 tests: schema parse for each action, schema rejects, system prompt persona prefix, user-message recency surfacing, stub fallback, parse-error fallback, hallucinated-id fallback, fence-stripping). `test/api/case-router-accept.test.ts` (7 tests: attach rebind + delete pending, open-new promote-in-place, override audit, 404 on missing run, 409 on already-accepted, 403 on non-author, 409 on signed). `test/workers/case-router-handler.test.ts` (5 tests: happy path + persona metadata, signed-note skip, missing-note drop, stub fallback persisted, agent throw retains audit + rethrows). `test/components/start-visit-dialog.test.tsx` rewritten to assert Sprint 0.13 behavior (default flow auto-posts with `caseManagementId: null`; forceCaseId binds explicitly).
  - **Files** (new): schema migration; `src/services/copilot/case-router.ts`; `src/workers/case-router.worker.ts` + `src/workers/case-router/handler.ts`; `src/app/api/notes/[id]/case-router/route.ts` + `…/accept/route.ts`; `src/app/(clinical)/review/[noteId]/_components/case-routing-panel.tsx`; 3 new test files.
  - **Files** (modified): `prisma/schema.prisma`; `src/lib/audit/actions.ts`; `src/lib/case-management/{validate,resolve}.ts`; `src/lib/encounters/start.ts`; `src/lib/queue.ts`; `src/workers/index.ts`; `src/workers/ai-generation/handler.ts`; `src/app/api/encounters/route.ts`; `src/app/api/schedules/[id]/start/route.ts`; `src/app/(clinical)/patients/[id]/_components/{start-visit-dialog,patient-chart-tabs,cases-panel}.tsx`; `src/app/(clinical)/review/[noteId]/{page.tsx,_components/review-client.tsx}`; `test/components/start-visit-dialog.test.tsx`.
  - **Locked decisions applied**: agent runs after AI-gen completes (BullMQ chain) → before review renders (decision 1); `Encounter.caseManagementId` stays NOT NULL (decision 2); routing settles at review, locked at sign (decision 3); override always one click (decision 4); confidence-gated UI weight (decision 5); Sonnet via Bedrock with Haiku fallback (decision 6); persona = `buildPersonaSystemBlock('chart')` + `PERSONA_ANTI_DRIFT_BLOCK` (decision 7); audit actions named per spec (decision 8); stub-mode synthesizes LOW-confidence proposal (decision 9); FHIR explicitly out of scope (decision 10); hero card retained (decision 11).
  - **Verify**: `npm run typecheck` clean; `npm test` 599/599 (added 26 tests); eslint clean on sprint-touched files; `npx prisma db seed` clean.
  - **Three-lens**: Clinician — one tap to start, record, one tap to confirm at review; case management becomes invisible until it needs attention; override always one tap; recording flow stops fragmenting attention with pre-recording case decisions. Compliance — every routing decision is captured end-to-end via `CaseRouterRun` (proposal + reasoning + confidence + model version) + the three audit actions (proposed/accepted/overridden). Auditor — `CaseRouterRun` is per-note source of truth for routing provenance; the audit triple is the per-event trail. A regulator can answer *"why is this note attached to this case?"* either way.

The "Open chart" / "Start note" buttons are removed: both already navigated to `/patients/[id]`, so the tappable row replaces them with no path lost. Unused `Button` import dropped. Desktop registry table untouched (already dense). Site name dropped from the mobile row to keep it to two clean lines.
  - **Episode cards (`episodes-panel.tsx`)**: `EpisodeCard` gains a `defaultExpanded` prop; `EpisodesPanel` passes `episodes.length === 1` — a lone episode stays open, 2+ collapse to header-only. The status badge (incl. `RECERT_DUE`) stays visible while collapsed, so the attention signal isn't buried.

- **2026-05-19 — Stripe-backed seat-licensing / subscriptions — Wave 7 Unit 38** (4-PR stack — `feat(billing): …`).
  - **Why**: 4.0 had a vestigial `Seat` model + a stub Stripe path but no real subscription flow — an org admin could neither buy seats nor assign them to clinicians. This is the real feature, ported from the OmniscribeThree design: one Stripe subscription per org, its line-item `quantity` = seat count, seats materialized by a webhook and assigned in-app.
  - **Schema (PR A)**: `Seat` gains `isActive` (the webhook soft-deactivates on downgrade/cancel — never hard-deletes) + `stripeSubId` (reconciliation key); new `SeatTransfer` model (append-only assign/reassign/revoke trail). Migration `20260519150000_seat_subscription_fields` — additive only. `src/lib/stripe/{env,client}.ts`; `stripe@22` dependency.
  - **Pipeline (PR B)**: `POST /api/billing/checkout` opens a Stripe Checkout Session stamped with `subscription_data.metadata.orgId`; `POST /api/webhooks/stripe` is the signature-verified sink and the ONLY path that creates `Seat` rows — `reconcileSeats` diffs subscription `quantity` against active seats and converges (create / reactivate / deactivate, never touching an assigned seat on downgrade); `POST /api/billing/portal` is the customer-portal redirect.
  - **Assignment + UI (PR C)**: `POST /api/admin/seats` is action-based — `assign` links a provisioned seat to a non-admin member (`OrgUser.seatId` + a `SeatTransfer`), `revoke` frees it. The legacy direct-allocate POST + `DELETE [id]` route are removed (seats are Stripe-owned now). `/admin/seats` is a working assign/revoke surface; `/admin/billing` (new) carries Subscribe + Manage-billing.
  - **Enforcement (PR D)**: `checkClinicianSeat` gates all three `startVisit` callers (`/api/encounters`, `/api/schedules/[id]/start`, `/api/admin/telehealth/sessions/[id]/start`) — a clinician needs an active assigned seat to create a note; ORG_ADMIN bypasses; the gate is **inert when Stripe is unconfigured** so dev / non-billing deploys are never blocked.
  - **Audit**: `STRIPE_CHECKOUT_STARTED`, `STRIPE_SUBSCRIPTION_UPDATED` / `_CANCELED`, `STRIPE_PAYMENT_FAILED`, `STRIPE_BILLING_PORTAL_OPENED`, `SEAT_ASSIGNED`. The owner-console seats route + the `services/billing/stripe.ts` stub are untouched (still used cross-org by the platform owner).
  - **Three-lens**: Clinician — recording access turns on the moment an admin assigns a seat. Compliance — `SeatTransfer` + the audit actions make license custody reconstructable. Auditor — seat lifecycle (Stripe provenance via `stripeSubId`, every assignment change, who-held-what-when) is traceable end to end.

- **2026-05-19 — Consolidate `OrgRole.SUPER_ADMIN` → `PlatformRole.PLATFORM_OWNER`** (follow-up — `refactor(authz): drop OrgRole.SUPER_ADMIN; ORG_ADMIN absorbs powers; platform-owner only via PlatformRole`).
  - **Why**: `OrgRole.SUPER_ADMIN` conflated two concepts that should be strictly separated: the platform owner (OmniScribe's owner — one person, global) and the customer's org admin (per-org). The role model is now: **platform owner** lives exclusively on `User.platformRole = PLATFORM_OWNER`; **org admin** lives exclusively on `OrgUser.role = ORG_ADMIN`. They never mix.
  - **Schema migration** (`20260519130000_drop_orgrole_super_admin`): hand-rolled enum-rebuild — backfilled `OrgUser` + `Invite` rows (SUPER_ADMIN → ORG_ADMIN), then RENAMEd the old type, CREATEd the new 4-value enum, ALTERed columns via `text` cast, DROPped the old type.
  - **Feature matrix** (`src/lib/authz/internal-authorization.ts`): SUPER_ADMIN row deleted. ORG_ADMIN absorbed every feature the deprecated role held — clinical lifecycle (NOTE_*, VOICE_ID, VISITS_CREATE, VOICE_PROFILE_MANAGE) on top of admin features (BILLING_MANAGE, TEAM_MEMBERS_MANAGE, TEMPLATE_*, TRANSCRIPT_VIEW). PATIENT_MANAGEMENT bypass logic now keys on ORG_ADMIN.
  - **Authz route bypasses**: `role !== 'SUPER_ADMIN'` → `role !== 'ORG_ADMIN'` across 11 note routes (sign, sections, stream, realtime-key, complete-stream, restyle, upload-audio, recording-state, paste-transcript, regenerate-section, transcript) + the FHIR-disconnect admin check + the telehealth preflight + telehealth room.
  - **ADMIN_ROLES sets** (3 layouts/pages + nav): SUPER_ADMIN dropped — set is now `{ORG_ADMIN, SITE_ADMIN}`. `src/lib/authz/server.ts` ADMIN_ROLES, `(admin)/layout.tsx`, `(admin)/admin/integrations/fhir/page.tsx`, `(clinical)/home/page.tsx`, `(clinical)/patients/page.tsx`, `components/app-nav.tsx`.
  - **Site-scope helpers** (`src/lib/authz/site-scope.ts`): `ALL_SITES_ROLES` is now `['ORG_ADMIN']`. `isAllSitesRole` returns true only for ORG_ADMIN.
  - **Provisioning paths**: `POST /api/owner/orgs` and `POST /api/auth/signup` assign `OrgRole.ORG_ADMIN` (was SUPER_ADMIN). UI label `new-org-form.tsx` updated.
  - **Invite + user PATCH whitelists**: `INVITABLE_ROLES` and `ASSIGNABLE_ROLES` are `[CLINICIAN, VIEWER, SITE_ADMIN]`. ORG_ADMIN never invitable (signup/owner-console only). Users picker shows friendly labels ("Clinician", "Non-clinician (read-only)", "Site admin").
  - **Seed**: `admin@demo.local` role SUPER_ADMIN → ORG_ADMIN. `owner@demo.local` stays as CLINICIAN + `platformRole=PLATFORM_OWNER` (the demo platform-owner persona).
  - **Tests**: 4 test files updated (`authz.test.ts`, `site-scope.test.ts`, `site-scope-filter.test.ts`, `encounters-site-enrollment.test.ts`). "SUPER_ADMIN can do everything" rewritten as "ORG_ADMIN can do everything (absorbed former SUPER_ADMIN powers)". Removed the now-contradictory "ORG_ADMIN gets team + billing, not clinical" assertion (ORG_ADMIN now has clinical).
  - **Docs**: `context/architecture.md` + `context/project-overview.md` updated to reflect the 4-role org model. Historical spec files (01, 08, 17, 37) left as-is — they describe what shipped at that point in time.
  - **Three-lens**: Clinician — no behavior change for clinicians; ORG_ADMIN founder retains full record-and-admin capability. Compliance — cleaner provenance; platform-level access is unambiguously PlatformRole, org-level is unambiguously OrgRole. Auditor — one less role to reason about; the privilege boundary is a straight line.

- **2026-05-19 — Profession-driven note division; drop `Patient.division`** (follow-up — `refactor(division): profession-driven note division; drop Patient.division`).
  - **Why**: A patient can see clinicians from multiple divisions across the same care arc (MD, PT, LCSW). The schema's `Patient.division` field was a vestigial fallback that reinforced the misconception that patients are bound to one division. The `/prepare` UI exposed Division as a clinician-editable knob while profession sat as a soft warning — inverted from the actual clinical rule that *the recording clinician's profession dictates the note type*.
  - **Schema**: `Patient.division` dropped (single-column `ALTER TABLE` migration `20260519120000_drop_patient_division`). No indexes referenced the column. `EpisodeOfCare.division` preserved (still clinical-scope-bearing). `Note.division` preserved (still locked at recording start; just sourced differently).
  - **Resolver**: `resolveDivisionForNote` rewritten — new signature takes `{ clinician: { professionType, division }, org }` (no `patient` arg). Precedence: `PROFESSION_TO_DIVISION[professionType]` → `clinician.division` (only reached when professionType is null; the gate refuses OTHER) → `org.defaultDivision` → `org.division` (when non-MULTI). `DivisionResolutionError` thrown on `OTHER` or unresolvable. `src/lib/encounters/start.ts` loads `clinicianOrgUser.{professionType,division}` inside the tx and passes them to the resolver; the 3 route callers (`/api/schedules/[id]/start`, `/api/encounters`, `/api/admin/telehealth/sessions/[id]/start`) catch `DivisionResolutionError` → 422 with `profession_other_blocked` / `no_division_resolvable` codes.
  - **Profession map**: `PROFESSION_TO_DIVISION` exported from `src/lib/professions.ts` covering all 13 enum values. MD/DO/NP/PA/RN → MEDICAL; OT/PT/SLP → REHAB; LCSW/LMFT/LPC/PSYCHOLOGIST → BEHAVIORAL_HEALTH; OTHER → null. `PROFESSION_OPTIONS` (profile-completion picker) now filters OTHER out; `/api/me/complete-profile` refuses OTHER server-side.
  - **Profile gate**: `requiresProfileCompletion` extended — `professionType === OTHER` now triggers the redirect to `/onboarding/profile`, same as null professionType.
  - **`VisitContextStrip`**: Division `<Select>` removed entirely. `TYPICAL_DIVISION_FOR_PROFESSION` map deleted (now load-bearing in `professions.ts`). Mismatch warning banner removed (no longer reachable). Top line is now read-only: "Recording as Dr. Park · PT → Rehab note". Template + Format pickers retained — still real clinician choices within a division.
  - **`/api/notes/[id]/visit-context`**: `division` field removed from PATCH body schema. `template_division_mismatch` validates against `note.division` (the locked value) instead of the now-deprecated body parameter.
  - **Patient surfaces**: Add Patient sheet drops Division dropdown; `/patients` list drops Division column + filter param; `<PatientIdentityHeader>` drops Division pill; `EpisodesPanel` drops `patientDivision` prop + "≠ patient" badge.
  - **Prompt builders / Copilot**: Note division read from `note.division` in all five sites (`build-prompt.ts`, `build-flag-analyzer-prompt.ts`, `build-brief-prompt.ts`, `projections.ts`, `copilot/tools.ts`). `projectPatientForPrompt` + `projectPatientForBrief` no longer carry `division`. `FlagAnalyzer.analyzeSection` takes an explicit `division: string` arg sourced from the note.
  - **Seed**: 3 demo patients + the Acme cross-org patient no longer set `division:` on `Patient.create`. EpisodeOfCare seeds still carry `division` (still required by the schema).
  - **Tests**: `division-resolve.test.ts` rewritten — 8 cases covering profession→division mapping (PT/MD/LCSW), OTHER throws, null professionType → clinician.division fallback, null/null → org.defaultDivision → org.division → throws. 6 other test files (`build-artifact-prompt`, `build-brief-prompt`, `build-brief-prompt-external-context`, `copilot-draft-tools`, `copilot-fhir-tools`, `platform-metrics`, `usage-rollup`) updated to drop division from patient/projection fixtures. 500/500 tests pass, typecheck clean, eslint clean.
  - **Three-lens**: Clinician — no pointless division picker; the note matches what the clinician is licensed to write. Compliance — note division traces deterministically to the recording clinician's profession, not a clinician-selectable knob. Auditor — one fewer degree of freedom; profession→division→template is a straight line.
